***ладонь.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ладонь.html>ладо́нь</a> (691)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Metathesis of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*dolnь</i>; the expected form <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">до́лонь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dólonʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> occurs dialectally. Doublet of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:длань.html>дла́нь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dlanʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, a borrowing from Old Church Slavonic.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ладонь.html>ладо́нь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ladónʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ладонь.html>ладо́ни</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ладонь.html>ладо́ни</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ладонь.html>ладо́ней</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>palm <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of the hand</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***ладоши.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ладоши.html>ладоши</a> (8698)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ладоши.html>ладо́ши</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ladóši</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr> <abbr title="plural number">pl</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ладоши.html>ладо́ш</a></b>, <i>plural only</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Diminutive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ладонь.html>ладо́ни</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ladóni</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>: palms of the hands
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бить.html>бить</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ладоши.html>ладо́ши</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">bitʹ v <b>ladóši</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to clap one’s hands</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хлопать.html>хло́пать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ладоши.html>ладо́ши</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">xlópatʹ v <b>ladóši</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to clap one’s hands</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***ладья.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ладья.html>ладья́</a> (16199)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*oldī</i>, cognate with modern Russian <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лодка.html>ло́дка</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">lódka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ладья.html>ладья́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ladʹjá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ладья.html>ладьи́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ладья.html>ладьи́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ладья.html>ладе́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> boat, longship <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">a type of medieval vessel propelled by oars and a sail</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>vase or other vessel in the form of a boat</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chess</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> rook, castle (Russian abbreviation: Л)</li></ol>

***ладящий.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ладить.html>ла́дящий</a> (14072)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ладить.html>ла́дящий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ládjaščij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">present active imperfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ладить.html>ла́дить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">láditʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лазер.html>ла́зер</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lázer, lázɛr</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:лазить.html>ла́зивший</a> (8759)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***лазить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:лазить.html>ла́зить</a> (8759)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*làziti</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лазить.html>ла́зить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">lázitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">пола́зить</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to climb, to clamber</li>
<li>to creep</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лазить.html>ла́зить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lázitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пола́зить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">polázitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> are Russian abstract verbs. Their counterparts, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лезть.html>лезть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">leztʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:полезть.html>поле́зть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">poléztʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, are concrete verbs.</li>
<li>The imperative forms <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лазить.html>ла́зь</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">lazʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> / <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лазить.html>ла́зьте</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">lázʹte</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (including derivatives with prefixes) are rarely used and considered illiterate, and are not recommended for use. The recommended imperative forms are suppletive forms <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">полеза́й</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">polezáj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> / <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">полеза́йте</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">polezájte</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><i>See also <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лезть.html>лезть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">leztʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> for verbal derivatives in <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">-леза́ть</span>.</i></li></ul>

***лазурь.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:лазурь.html>лазу́рь</a> (29368)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">lazur</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лазурь.html>лазу́рь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">lazúrʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лазурь.html>лазу́ри</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лазурь.html>лазу́ри</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лазурь.html>лазу́рей</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:лайка.html>ла́йка</a> (16066)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лай.html>лай</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">laj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лайка.html>ла́йка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">lájka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лайка.html>ла́йки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лайка.html>ла́йки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лайка.html>ла́ек</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Laika (<i>lit.</i>, barker), a native Russian breed of dog, a rather small hunting dog of Russia’s northern forests, similar to a husky</li>
<li>kidskin, kid leather</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:лак.html>лак</a> (6581)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Lack</i> or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">lak</i> or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">laque</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Persian language">Persian</a></span> <i class="fa-Arab mention" lang="fa">لاک</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="fa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lāk</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hindi" class="extiw" title="w:Hindi">Hindi</a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="hi">लाख</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="hi-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lākh</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sanskrit" class="extiw" title="w:Sanskrit">Sanskrit</a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="sa">लाक्षा</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lākṣā</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***лакать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:лакать.html>лака́ть</a> (24730)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*lokati</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лакать.html>лака́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">lakátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">вы́лакать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to lap <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to take liquid into the mouth with the tongue</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to drink greedily or in large amounts (usually alcohol)</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лак.html>лак</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lak</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-овый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лаковый.html>ла́ковый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">lákovyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>lacquered
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:лаковый.html>ла́ковая</a></b> кера́мика</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>lákovaja</b> kerámika</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>lacquered</b> ceramic</span></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лакированный.html>лакиро́ванный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">lakiróvannyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> lacquer, varnish
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:лаковый.html>ла́ковое</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дерево.html>де́рево</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>lákovoje</b> dérevo</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Chinese_lacquer_tree" class="extiw" title="w:Chinese lacquer tree">Chinese <b>lacquer</b> tree</a>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/varnish_tree" class="extiw" title="w:varnish tree"><b>varnish</b> tree</a> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content"><span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Toxicodendron_vernicifluum" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Toxicodendron vernicifluum"><i>Toxicodendron vernicifluum</i></a></span></span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***лакомый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:лакомый.html>ла́комый</a> (19758)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*olkomъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лакомый.html>ла́комый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">lákomyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)ла́комее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)ла́комей</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:самый.html>са́мый</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лакомый.html>ла́комый</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>dainty, tasty
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:лакомый.html>ла́комое</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:блюдо.html>блю́до</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>lákomoje</b> bljúdo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">dainty dish</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:лакомый.html>ла́комый</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:кусок.html>кусо́к</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>lákomyj</b> kusók</i> ― <span class="e-translation">titbit; tasty morsel</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>fond (of); partial (to) (especially food)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:лакомый.html>ла́кома</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:кошка.html>ко́шка</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рыбка.html>ры́бки</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:да.html>да</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вода.html>во́ду</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лезть.html>лезть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хотеться.html>хо́чется</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>lákoma</b> kóška do rýbki, da v vódu leztʹ ne xóčetsja</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">all cats love fish but fear to wet their paws</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

***лама.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:лама.html>ла́ма</a> (21315)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Spanish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Spanish language">Spanish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="es">llama</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Quechuan_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Quechuan languages">Quechua</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="qu">llama</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лама.html>ла́ма</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">láma</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лама.html>ла́мы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лама.html>ла́мы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лама.html>лам</a></b>)
</p>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Standard_Tibetan" class="extiw" title="w:Standard Tibetan">Tibetan</a></span> <i class="Tibt mention" lang="bo">བླ་མ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="bo-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bla ma</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:лампа.html>ла́мпа</a> (2116)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лампа.html>ла́мпа</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">lámpa</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лампа.html>ла́мпы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лампа.html>ла́мпы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лампа.html>ла́мп</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>lamp
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">светодио́дная <b><a href = vnd.unilang:лампа.html>ла́мпа</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">svetodiódnaja <b>lámpa</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">LED <b>lamp</b></span></div></dd>
